msg:Recently, I had the honor of traveling in Xiangyang and chose Xiangyang Xinglan Ramada Hotel as my place to stay. From the moment I checked in, I was deeply attracted by the excellent service and elegant environment of this hotel.
First of all, I would like to praise the environment of the hotel. The whole hotel is uniquely designed and full of modern and luxurious a**osphere. The lobby is spacious and bright, giving people a feeling of being at home. And every corner of the hotel reveals quietness and comfort, which is an ideal place to relax.
Especially the sound insulation of the room is surprisingly good. At night, I can hardly hear the noise outside and can enjoy a quiet night. The design of the room also fully considers the needs of the guests, and all kinds of facilities are available, and they all maintain extremely high quality.
The service of the front desk reception also impressed me. The young lady is warm and thoughtful. Not only did she provide me with a detailed travel guide, but she also took the initiative to ask about my needs to ensure that I was satisfied every moment in the hotel. This meticulous service made me feel the reception level of Xiangyang's high-end brand.
Of course, breakfast is also a highlight that I have to mention. The hotel has a rich variety of breakfasts, with all kinds of Chinese and Western cuisine. I particularly like their Xiangyang beef noodles, the noodles are chewy and the soup is rich, which is really memorable. The Wuhan hot dry noodles are also very authentic, and every bite makes me feel the taste of my hometown.
What surprised me most was that the view of the room was very good. Standing in front of the window, I can see the beautiful scenery of Xiangzhou District, which undoubtedly adds a lot of fun to my trip.
Overall, Xiangyang Xinglan Ramada Hotel provided me with an excellent experience beyond my expectations. Whether it is the environment, service or facilities, I am very satisfied. I believe that whether it is a business trip or a tourist vacation, choosing Xiangyang Xinglan Ramada Hotel is a wise choice.

name:X‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçf‚Äçu‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçh‚Äçu‚Äçi‚Äçy‚Äça‚Äço‚Äçd‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçd‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in October 2021
info:Couples
info:40 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted October 9, 2021
msg:Environment: The hotel is not in the center of Xiangyang, so it is suitable for driving. It takes about half an hour to reach the ancient city or Tangcheng. Next to the hotel is a shopping mall that doesn't look so good, but there are McDonald's, movie theaters, Decathlon, some restaurants, and large supermarkets. There are not many local specialties in the shopping places for locals, but most of them are foreign flavors, so eating nearby is not recommended. But shopping has everything you need.
Parking: Free parking is available on the ground in front of the hotel, and the parking spaces are basically sufficient. Remember to scan the QR code and enter the license plate when you go out every day.
Service: The check-in and check-out speed is very fast, and the front desk can collect express delivery. The room attendants are friendly and happy to ask for more water.
Breakfast: It belongs to the domestic five-star medium-to-upper level. It has everything that should be found. It is more Chinese style. It is good except for the rich western pastries that are not as rich as the international five-star. There are many tourists during the holidays, but the waiter takes the table quickly. The Xiangyang beef noodles in the breakfast restaurant is delicious. Compared with the taste of the most famous local beef noodle shop, there is basically no difference. Breakfast until ten o'clock can meet the needs of most people.
Room: The room is very large, probably because it is assigned to the top one, with two large floor-to-ceiling windows, and the view is very good. There is a bathtub to soak in. The bedding is quite comfortable. There are too many glass in the room and it will be hot in summer. The waiter gave us an extra room card in advance to remind us that we need to turn on the air conditioner 24 hours a day to avoid the room being too hot when we come back from the outside after the power outage.
Gym: The facilities are relatively complete, as well as table tennis and billiards. The gym is open 24 hours.
Disadvantages: The hotel has a high floor and a lot of rooms. Four families get married at the same time every day in the banquet hall left behind during the National Day holiday. As a result, the four elevators are seriously insufficient between 10:00 and 12:00. A large number of wedding guests and guests Passengers use the elevator together, the efficiency of the elevator is very low, and sometimes it is impossible to get on the elevator after waiting for a long time. It is suggested that in this case, two elevators can be used exclusively for sending hotel guests, and two are used for wedding banquets to improve the efficiency of elevators. After staying for three days, the tea in the room was exhausted, but the waiter did not replenish it. Many parents bring their children to play in the gym. The gym is quite noisy, and some garbage discarded in the gym has not been cleaned up for a long time. It is recommended to have a special person to clean it regularly and strengthen some management. It is not safe for children who are too young to run around in the gym and play equipment by themselves.
In general, it is suitable for family travel and travel.
